versioning and migration through a multi-layered architecture spanning backend Go code and frontend TypeScript. The migration system supports dashboard schema versions 0-42, with version 42 being the final version for the v1 dashboard API.\\n\\n## Core Migration Infrastructure (apps/dashboard/pkg/migration/)\\n\\nThe main migration orchestrator is in **migrate.go**, which implements the `Migrate()` function that manages the complete migration pipeline. It performs sequential steps: cleanup of backend-only properties, application of frontend defaults, panel defaults assignment, unique ID generation, and then executes individual schema version migrations.\\n\\nThe **migrations.go** file in the schemaversion package defines the `SchemaVersionMigrationFunc` type and the `GetMigrations()` registry that returns a map of all version migrations (v2-v42). It also provides utility functions like `GetSchemaVersion()` to extract and normalize schema versions from dashboard JSON.\\n\\n## Field-Level Migration Functions (apps/dashboard/pkg/migration/schemaversion/)\\n\\nIndividual schema version migrations are implemented as separate files (v2.go through v42.go, totaling 41 migration functions). Key migrations include:\\n\\n- **V2**: Handles legacy services.filter structure migrations\\n- **V6**: Moves dropdown annotations to new schema\\n- **V7**: Converts nav property to timepicker\\n- **V9**: Removes first threshold value from singlestat panel thresholds\\n- **V14**: Migrates sharedCrosshair boolean to graphTooltip integer\\n- **V16**: Implements the row-based to grid-based layout migration (the largest migration)\\n- **V28**: Performs variable and panel transformation updates\\n- **V33**: Handles DataSource reference migrations with DataSourceInfoProvider\\n- **V36**: Updates panel options and field configurations\\n- **V38**: Migrates table display modes to cell options\\n- **V41 & V42**: Final schema version updates\\n\\nUtility functions in **migration_utils.go** provide type-safe value extraction from maps, including `GetStringValue()`, `GetBoolValue()`, `GetIntValue()`, and `GetFloatValue()`, ensuring consistent handling of type conversions throughout migrations.\\n\\n## Frontend Defaults Application\\n\\nThe **frontend_defaults.go** file applies all DashboardModel and PanelModel constructor defaults before migrations run, matching the frontend's behavior. This includes default values for title, timezone, time range, panels, targets, and grid positions. The `applyPanelDefaults()` function ensures every panel has baseline properties like gridPos and targets.\\n\\n## API Version Conversion\\n\\nThe conversion subsystem in **apps/dashboard/pkg/migration/conversion/** handles cross-version API conversions between v0alpha1, v1beta1, v2alpha1, and v2beta1 dashboard types. **conversion.go** registers conversion functions between all API version pairs, while individual conversion files (v0.go, v1.go, v2.go, v2alpha1_to_v2beta1.go) implement the actual conversion logic using Kubernetes conversion scopes.\\n\\n## Schema Definitions\\n\\nDashboard API schema definitions are versioned in **apps/dashboard/pkg/apis/dashboard/**:\\n- **v0alpha1, v1beta1, v2alpha1, v2beta1**: Each contains types.go, constants.go, dashboard_spec.go for their respective API versions\\n- **types.go & utils.go** in the parent directory provide shared types and utilities\\n- **apps/dashboard/pkg/apis/dashboard/v0alpha1/dashboard_spec.go** and similar files contain the actual spec definitions\\n\\nThe **HandoffSchemaVersion** constant (value 36) defined in **pkg/kinds/dashboard/addenda.go** marks the minimum schema version at which the Thema-based schema becomes valid. Dashboards below this version require the TypeScript migration logic to run first.\\n\\n## Error Handling and Metrics\\n\\n**errors.go** defines MigrationError and MinimumVersionError types for comprehensive error reporting. **metrics.go** tracks migration success and failure metrics with counters for dashboard migrations.\\n\\n## Test Infrastructure\\n\\nEach schema version migration has corresponding test files (v2_test.go through v42_test.go). The **testutil/** directory provides mock objects and utilities for testing. Test data is stored in testdata/ subdirectories for comprehensive coverage of various migration scenarios.\\n\\n## DataSource Handling\\n\\n**datasource_utils.go** provides utilities for handling DataSource references during migrations, supporting the DataSourceInfoProvider interface for context-aware migrations (particularly in v33 and v36).\\n\\nThis architecture ensures consistency between frontend and backend migrations, with all 41 field-level migrations defined as Go functions that match the logic in the TypeScript DashboardMigrator class, allowing seamless dashboard JSON upgrades from legacy versions to the current schema version 42.\"\n}\n"},"caller":{"type":"direct"}}],"stop_reason":null,"stop_sequence":null,"usage":{"input_tokens":9,"cache_creation_input_tokens":1752,"cache_read_input_tokens":70833,"cache_creation":{"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":0,"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":1752},"output_tokens":1,"service_tier":"standard","inference_geo":"not_available"},"context_management":null},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"c21512d4-bab6-4c67-b3de-25dd75029519","uuid":"e7d73aaa-ac3f-4907-8d56-b9d58e18936c"}

versioning and migration through a multi-layered architecture spanning backend Go code and frontend TypeScript. The migration system supports dashboard schema versions 0-42, with version 42 being the final version for the v1 dashboard API.\\n\\n## Core Migration Infrastructure (apps/dashboard/pkg/migration/)\\n\\nThe main migration orchestrator is in **migrate.go**, which implements the `Migrate()` function that manages the complete migration pipeline. It performs sequential steps: cleanup of backend-only properties, application of frontend defaults, panel defaults assignment, unique ID generation, and then executes individual schema version migrations.\\n\\nThe **migrations.go** file in the schemaversion package defines the `SchemaVersionMigrationFunc` type and the `GetMigrations()` registry that returns a map of all version migrations (v2-v42). It also provides utility functions like `GetSchemaVersion()` to extract and normalize schema versions from dashboard JSON.\\n\\n## Field-Level Migration Functions (apps/dashboard/pkg/migration/schemaversion/)\\n\\nIndividual schema version migrations are implemented as separate files (v2.go through v42.go, totaling 41 migration functions). Key migrations include:\\n\\n- **V2**: Handles legacy services.filter structure migrations\\n- **V6**: Moves dropdown annotations to new schema\\n- **V7**: Converts nav property to timepicker\\n- **V9**: Removes first threshold value from singlestat panel thresholds\\n- **V14**: Migrates sharedCrosshair boolean to graphTooltip integer\\n- **V16**: Implements the row-based to grid-based layout migration (the largest migration)\\n- **V28**: Performs variable and panel transformation updates\\n- **V33**: Handles DataSource reference migrations with DataSourceInfoProvider\\n- **V36**: Updates panel options and field configurations\\n- **V38**: Migrates table display modes to cell options\\n- **V41 & V42**: Final schema version updates\\n\\nUtility functions in **migration_utils.go** provide type-safe value extraction from maps, including `GetStringValue()`, `GetBoolValue()`, `GetIntValue()`, and `GetFloatValue()`, ensuring consistent handling of type conversions throughout migrations.\\n\\n## Frontend Defaults Application\\n\\nThe **frontend_defaults.go** file applies all DashboardModel and PanelModel constructor defaults before migrations run, matching the frontend's behavior. This includes default values for title, timezone, time range, panels, targets, and grid positions. The `applyPanelDefaults()` function ensures every panel has baseline properties like gridPos and targets.\\n\\n## API Version Conversion\\n\\nThe conversion subsystem in **apps/dashboard/pkg/migration/conversion/** handles cross-version API conversions between v0alpha1, v1beta1, v2alpha1, and v2beta1 dashboard types. **conversion.go** registers conversion functions between all API version pairs, while individual conversion files (v0.go, v1.go, v2.go, v2alpha1_to_v2beta1.go) implement the actual conversion logic using Kubernetes conversion scopes.\\n\\n## Schema Definitions\\n\\nDashboard API schema definitions are versioned in **apps/dashboard/pkg/apis/dashboard/**:\\n- **v0alpha1, v1beta1, v2alpha1, v2beta1**: Each contains types.go, constants.go, dashboard_spec.go for their respective API versions\\n- **types.go & utils.go** in the parent directory provide shared types and utilities\\n- **apps/dashboard/pkg/apis/dashboard/v0alpha1/dashboard_spec.go** and similar files contain the actual spec definitions\\n\\nThe **HandoffSchemaVersion** constant (value 36) defined in **pkg/kinds/dashboard/addenda.go** marks the minimum schema version at which the Thema-based schema becomes valid. Dashboards below this version require the TypeScript migration logic to run first.\\n\\n## Error Handling and Metrics\\n\\n**errors.go** defines MigrationError and MinimumVersionError types for comprehensive error reporting. **metrics.go** tracks migration success and failure metrics with counters for dashboard migrations.\\n\\n## Test Infrastructure\\n\\nEach schema version migration has corresponding test files (v2_test.go through v42_test.go). The **testutil/** directory provides mock objects and utilities for testing.
